//==&gt;   A programmer les heures sous le format &quot;hh:mm:ss&quot;

var heure_debut_pocedure_A = &quot;05:40:00&quot;;

var heure_fin_pocedure_A = &quot;13:00:00&quot;;

//=======================    fin des programmations

var Date_machine = new Date();
var Day = Date_machine.getDate();
var Month = Date_machine.getMonth()+1;
var Year = Date_machine.getFullYear();

if (Day.toString().length == 1)
Day = '0'+Day;
if (Month.toString().length == 1)
Month = '0'+Month;

var Date_heure_debut_pocedure_A = Day+&quot;/&quot;+Month+&quot;/&quot;+Year+&quot; &quot;+heure_debut_pocedure_A;
var Date_heure_fin_pocedure_A = Day+&quot;/&quot;+Month+&quot;/&quot;+Year+&quot; &quot;+heure_fin_pocedure_A;</subParameter>

//===  A programmer

var heure_debut_attente = &quot;05:30:00&quot;;        //        hh:mm:ss

var heure_fin_attente = &quot;06:50:00&quot;;        //        hh:mm:ss

//======================= fin des programations

var Date_machine = new Date();
var Day = Date_machine.getDate();
var Month = Date_machine.getMonth()+1;
var Year = Date_machine.getFullYear();

if (Day.toString().length == 1)
Day = '0'+Day;
if (Month.toString().length == 1)
Month = '0'+Month;

var Date_Heure_debut_attente = Day+&quot;/&quot;+Month+&quot;/&quot;+Year+&quot; &quot;+heure_debut_attente;
var Date_Heure_fin_attente = Day+&quot;/&quot;+Month+&quot;/&quot;+Year+&quot; &quot;+heure_fin_attente;</subParameter>
